<p><i><font color="#007F00">All versions (1 - 40) and all error correction levels</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">(L, M, Q, H) are supported.</font></i></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> (pX + sQZSize - </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000">) * </font><font color="#00007F">4</font><font color="#000000"> + </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> + (pY - </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> + sQZSize) * </font><font color="#00007F">4</font><font color="#000000"> * sImgSize </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tPos</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tVal </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> tPos </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tPos + </font><font color="#00007F">3</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sImgData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># update symbol map</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> pX + (pY - </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000">) * sQRSize </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sSymbolMap</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># update data map</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pColor = </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tVal <b>else</b> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tVal</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tVal </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> pX + (pY - </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000">) * sQRSize </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sDataMap</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> _draw</font></p>
<p></p>

<p><b><font color="#000000">private</font></b><font color="#000000"> <b>function</b> _format pData, pLen</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tPad</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> pLen - </font><font color="#7F007F">length</font><font color="#000000">(pData) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tPad</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tPad &gt; </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>repeat</b> tPad</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"0"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">before</font><font color="#000000"> pData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>

<p><b><font color="#000000">private</font></b><font color="#000000"> <b>function</b> _int pAlpha</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pAlpha = </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> pAlpha </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sGF256List</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">charToNum</font><font color="#000000">(tChar) &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">comma</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">after</font><font color="#000000"> tVals</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">delete</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> -1 </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tVals</font></p>

<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">private</font></b><font color="#000000"> <b>function</b> _errorCodes pByteStream, pNumErrorCodes</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tNumDataCodes, tTotalCodes, tRefExp, tExp, tErrorCodeA, tMsgPolyA</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">length</font><font color="#000000">(pByteStream) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tNumDataCodes</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tNumDataCodes + pNumErrorCodes </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tTotalCodes</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tTotalCodes - </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tRefExp</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tRefExp </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tExp</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorCodeA</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># store the message polynomial coefficients</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tMsgPolyA</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">with</font><font color="#000000"> i = </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tNumDataCodes</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">charToNum</font><font color="#000000">(</font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> i </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> pByteStream) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorCodeA[tExp]</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">subtract</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">from</font><font color="#000000"> tExp</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># zero fill the remaining coefficients</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">with</font><font color="#000000"> i = tExp </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">step</font><font color="#000000"> -1</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorCodeA[i]</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># protect from infinite loop</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tSanity</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tSanity</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># get the generator polynomial exponents</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tLine</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">lineOffset</font><font color="#000000">(</font><font color="#7F007F">LF</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; pNumErrorCodes, </font><font color="#7F007F">LF</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; sGenPolyAlphaExpList) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tLine</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tGenData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tLine </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sGenPolyAlphaExpList </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tGenData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tGenExp</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> -1 </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tGenData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tGenExp</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tGenExpCount</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">num</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">items</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> tGenExp </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tGenExpCount</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">until</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">num</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">lines</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">keys</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorCodeA = pNumErrorCodes </font><font color="#7F007F">or</font><font color="#000000"> tSanity &gt; </font><font color="#00007F">1000</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">add</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tSanity</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># first coefficient alpha value: to add to all the generator alpha values</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tRefAlpha</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> _alpha(tErrorCodeA[tRefExp]) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tRefAlpha</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">with</font><font color="#000000"> i = </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tGenExpCount</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tECIndex, tGenAlpha</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tRefExp - i + </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tECIndex</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> i </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tGenExp </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tGenAlpha</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># calculate the new coefficient value</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> _int((tRefAlpha + tGenAlpha) </font><font color="#7F007F">mod</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">255</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">bitXOr</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorCodeA[tECIndex] </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorCodeA[tECIndex]</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># remove leading zero coefficients</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">with</font><font color="#000000"> i = tRefExp </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">step</font><font color="#000000"> -1</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>if</b> tErrorCodeA[i] = </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">delete</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">variable</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorCodeA[i]</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">subtract</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">from</font><font color="#000000"> tRefExp</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            <b>exit</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tKeys</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">keys</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorCodeA </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tKeys</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">sort</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">lines</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tKeys </font><font color="#7F007F">descending</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">numeric</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tErrorBytes</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">numToChar</font><font color="#000000">(tErrorCodeA[tKey]) </font><font color="#7F007F">after</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorBytes</font></p>

<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">/**</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Create a QR code</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Example:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">qrCreate "MyImage", "QR data", "M", 3</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Example: </font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">--creating QR Code with ECC level M, Size 3, Mask 7 and version 14</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">qrCreate "MyImage", "QR data", "M", 3, 7, 14, 14</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Example:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">-- example how to use qrCreate with LiveCode server</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">qrCreate "!", tData, tECC, tSize</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">put the result into tData</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">if tData begins with "Error" then</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put tData</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">else</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   # line 1 of the result contains some info</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   # the remaining lines contain the png image data</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put line 1 of tData into tInfo</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   delete line 1 of tData</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put "&amp;lt;b&amp;gt;Qr code info&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br/&amp;gt;" &amp; LF</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put "Version: " &amp; item 1 of tInfo &amp; "&amp;lt;br/&amp;gt;" &amp; LF</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put "ECC: " &amp; item 2 of tInfo &amp; "&amp;lt;br/&amp;gt;" &amp; LF</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put "Mode: " &amp; item 3 of tInfo &amp; "&amp;lt;br/&amp;gt;" &amp; LF</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put "Mask: " &amp; item 4 of tInfo &amp; "&amp;lt;br/&amp;gt;" &amp; LF</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   # show the image</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put base64Encode(tData) into tData</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   replace LF with empty in tData</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">   put "&amp;lt;img src='data:image/png;base64," &amp; tData &amp; "'/&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br/&amp;gt;" &amp; LF</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">end if</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Description:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Set the text of an image to a QR code or get the PMG data of the QR code image.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Parameters:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pImg:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">The name of an image object on the card, a filename or the special code "!" which</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">will return the image data in the result.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pData:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">The data to be encoded.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pECC (enum):</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">The error correction level</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- "L" : 7% error correction</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- "M" : 15% error correction</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- "Q" : 25% error correction</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- "H" : 30% error correction</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pSize (integer):</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Module size you can make the code larger/smaller.  You can also just</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">rescale the image after the code has been created.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pMask (integer):</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">An integer value between 0 and 7. When encoding a QR code, there are</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">eight mask patterns that you can use to change the outputted matrix.</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Each mask pattern changes the bits according to their coordinates in</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">the QR matrix. The purpose of a mask pattern is to make the QR code</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">easier for a QR scanner to read.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pMinVersion:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">An integer value between 1 and 40. It must be lower or equal to pMaxVersion.</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">If pMinVersion is not specified then the default value of 1 is used.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pMaxVersion:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">An integer value between 1 and 40. It must be higher or equal to pMinVersion.</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">If pMaxVersion is not specified then the default value of 40 is used.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">The result:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">If successful, the first line of the result will be the following values: </font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- QR version</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- ECC</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- Mode</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- Mask</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">- Image size with quiet zone (based on module size 1)</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">If there was an error the result will contain "Error:" and then an error</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">description.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">If the special character '!' is used for pImg, then the result also</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">contains the raw output of a png image.  You can use this data, for example,</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">with LiveCode server to generate QR codes on web pages.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">*/</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> qrCreate pImg, pData, pECC, pSize, pMask, pMinVersion, pMaxVersion</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">lock</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">screen</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>try</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># check target image object exists</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tPNG</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">there</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">an</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">img</font><font color="#000000"> pImg <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">long</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">id</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">img</font><font color="#000000"> pImg </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> pImg</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">false</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tPNG</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">exists</font><font color="#000000">(pImg) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tPNG</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># check ECC</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000">(pECC </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">among</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">items</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"L,M,Q,H"</font><font color="#000000">) <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">throw</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"ECC must be L, M, Q or H"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> pECC </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sECC</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># min version, max version, numeric mode, alpha mode, 8-bit mode, Kanji mode</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">matchText</font><font color="#000000">(pData, </font><font color="#00007F">"^[[:digit:]]+$"</font><font color="#000000">) = </font><font color="#7F007F">true</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> sModeNumeric </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>else</b> <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">matchText</font><font color="#000000">(pData, </font><font color="#00007F">"^["</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; sAlphaChars &amp; </font><font color="#00007F">"]+$"</font><font color="#000000">) = </font><font color="#7F007F">true</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> sModeAlpha </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> sModeByte </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># parameters OK - start timimg</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tMillisecs</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">millisecs</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tMillisecs</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tDataLength</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">length</font><font color="#000000">(pData) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tDataLength</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># calculate minimum version required</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tMinVersion</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tMinVersion</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> pMinVersion </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b> </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> pMinVersion</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> pMaxVersion </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b> </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">40</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> pMaxVersion</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> pMaxVersion &gt; </font><font color="#00007F">40</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">or</font><font color="#000000"> pMaxVersion &lt; </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">or</font><font color="#000000"> pMinVersion &lt; </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">or</font><font color="#000000"> pMinVersion &gt; </font><font color="#00007F">40</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">throw</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"allowed values for pMinVersion to pMaxVersion are 1 to 40"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> pMinVersion &gt; pMaxVersion <b>then</b> </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">throw</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"pMinversion must be lower or equal to pMaxVersion"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">     </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">with</font><font color="#000000"> tVersion = pMinVersion </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> pMaxVersion</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tCCIBits, tBitStreamLength, tErrorWords, tTotalWords, tBitStreamMax, tRemBits</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIBits </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- character count indicator</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBitStreamLength</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">for</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">each</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIData </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> sCCIList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            <b>if</b> tVersion &gt;= </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIData </font><font color="#7F007F">and</font><font color="#000000"> tVersion &lt;= </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIData <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#007F00"># total data codewords and error codewords</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tVersion </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sCapacityList </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tTotalWords</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">itemOffset</font><font color="#000000">(sECC, </font><font color="#00007F">"L,M,Q,H"</font><font color="#000000">) + </font><font color="#00007F">3</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tVersion </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sCapacityList </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorWords</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#007F00"># maximum bit stream length for version &amp; EEC</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> (tTotalWords - tErrorWords) * </font><font color="#00007F">8</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBitStreamMax</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#007F00"># use CCI for correct mode</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               <b>switch</b> sMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                  <b>case</b> sModeNumeric</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">3</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIBits</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> ((tDataLength </font><font color="#7F007F">mod</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">3</font><font color="#000000">) + </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"0,4,7"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tRemBits</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">4</font><font color="#000000"> + tCCIBits + (</font><font color="#00007F">10</font><font color="#000000"> * (tDataLength </font><font color="#7F007F">div</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">3</font><font color="#000000">)) + tRemBits </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBitStreamLength</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">break</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                  <b>case</b> sModeAlpha</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">4</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIBits</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">4</font><font color="#000000"> + tCCIBits + (</font><font color="#00007F">11</font><font color="#000000"> * (tDataLength </font><font color="#7F007F">div</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000">)) + (</font><font color="#00007F">6</font><font color="#000000"> * (tDataLength </font><font color="#7F007F">mod</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000">)) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBitStreamLength</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">break</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                  <b>case</b> sModeByte</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">5</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tCCIBits</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">4</font><font color="#000000"> + tCCIBits + (</font><font color="#00007F">8</font><font color="#000000"> * tDataLength) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBitStreamLength</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                     </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">break</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               <b>end</b> <b>switch</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#007F00"># check if data fits in current version </font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               <b>if</b> tBitStreamLength &gt; </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">and</font><font color="#000000"> tBitStreamLength &lt;= tBitStreamMax <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                  </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tVersion </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tMinVersion</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                  <b>exit</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># check if we have already found the minimum version</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>if</b> tMinVersion &gt; </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            <b>exit</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> tMinVersion = </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># too much data even for version 40</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">throw</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Data too large for QRCode"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tMinVersion </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sVersion</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># create the data bit stream</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>switch</b> sMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>case</b> sModeNumeric</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tData, tLength, tBits</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#007F00"># add numeric mode indicator and CCI to bit stream</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"0001"</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; _format(</font><font color="#7F007F">baseConvert</font><font color="#000000">(tDataLength, </font><font color="#00007F">10</font><font color="#000000">, </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000">), tCCIBits) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sBitStream</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">until</font><font color="#000000"> pData = </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">3</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> pData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">length</font><font color="#000000">(tData) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tLength</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">delete</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tLength </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> pData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> tLength </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"4,7,10"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBits</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> _format(</font><font color="#7F007F">baseConvert</font><font color="#000000">(tData, </font><font color="#00007F">10</font><font color="#000000">, </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000">), tBits) </font><font color="#7F007F">after</font><font color="#000000"> sBitStream</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">break</font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> pData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">length</font><font color="#000000">(tData) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tLength</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">delete</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tLength </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> pData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               <b>if</b> tLength = </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                  </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">offset</font><font color="#000000">(</font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tData, sAlphaChars) - </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tVal1</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                  </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">offset</font><font color="#000000">(</font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tData, sAlphaChars) - </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tVal2</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">                  </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> _format(</font><font color="#7F007F">baseConvert</font><font color="#000000">(tVal1 * </font><font color="#00007F">45</font><font color="#000000">+ tVal2, </font><font color="#00007F">10</font><font color="#000000">, </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000">), </font><font color="#00007F">11</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBinary</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">                  </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> _format(</font><font color="#7F007F">baseConvert</font><font color="#000000">(tVal1, </font><font color="#00007F">10</font><font color="#000000">, </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000">), </font><font color="#00007F">6</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBinary</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">lineOffset</font><font color="#000000">(</font><font color="#7F007F">LF</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; tCode, </font><font color="#7F007F">LF</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; sECCDataList) </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sECCDataList </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tECCData</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBlockIndex</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tDataBlockA</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorBlockA</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">for</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">each</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> tBlockCountIndex </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"3,6"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> tBlockCountIndex </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tECCData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBlocks</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> tBlockCountIndex + </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tECCData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tTotalWords</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> tBlockCountIndex + </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tECCData </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tDataWords</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tTotalWords - tDataWords </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorWords</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            <b>repeat</b> tBlocks</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">add</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tBlockIndex</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tDataWords </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sByteStream </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tDataBlockA[tBlockIndex]</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">delete</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">char</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> tDataWords </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sByteStream</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">               </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> _errorCodes(tDataBlockA[tBlockIndex], tErrorWords) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tErrorBlockA[tBlockIndex]</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># construct the final codeword sequence</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">length</font><font color="#000000">(tDataBlockA[tBlockIndex]) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tDataLength </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- last data blocks will always be of longest length</font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sByteStream</font></p>

<p><i><font color="#007F00">/**</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Set colors other than the default black and white</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Example:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">qrSetColors "Blue", "Yellow"</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Parameters:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pForeground (string):</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">A color name or RGB triplet</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">pBackground (string):</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">A color name or RGB triplet</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Description:</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">Optionally use colors other than black and white there must be a high</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">enough contrast between colors for scanning the foreground color</font></i></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">should be darker than the background color.</font></i></p>
<p></p>
<p><i><font color="#007F00">*/</font></i></p>
